#Setup
asoiaf_destroy_crownlands_title_effect = {
	destroy_title = title:k_the_crownlands
}

asoiaf_religion_doctrines_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_game_rule = default_gender_equality }
		faith:old_gods_wnw = {
			remove_doctrine = doctrine_gender_equal
			add_doctrine = doctrine_gender_male_dominated #male dominated in the Seven Kingdoms
		}
		faith:valyrian_pan_freehold = {
			remove_doctrine = doctrine_gender_equal
			add_doctrine = doctrine_gender_male_dominated #evidence points to male dominance
		}
	}
	faith:old_gods_wnw = {
		remove_doctrine = doctrine_consanguinity_cousins
		add_doctrine = doctrine_consanguinity_aunt_nephew_and_uncle_niece #examples exist of northmen marrying nieces
	}
	faith:rhllor_fots = { #Red God is based on the faith followed by Stannis and his supporters, which was 100% fundamentalist
		remove_doctrine = doctrine_pluralism_righteous
		add_doctrine = doctrine_pluralism_fundamentalist
	}
	#faith:fots_seven = {
	#	remove_doctrine = doctrine_consanguinity_cousins
	#	add_doctrine = doctrine_consanguinity_aunt_nephew_and_uncle_niece #no evidence it's not accepted, but the lack of evidence isn't enough for now
	#}
}

		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_alive = yes is_landed = yes }

asoiaf_setup_characters_effect = {
	#every_living_character = { #Red Priest amulet startup effect
	#	limit = {
	#		AND = { #Red priest conditions; replace with the red priest trait once it's added
	#			has_trait = devoted
	#			religion = religion:the_rhllor_religion
	#		}
	#		#add exclusion for Thoros of Myr when he's got a custom ID
	#	}
	#	create_artifact_asoiaf_red_priest_necklace_effect = { OWNER = this }
	#}
	character:Targaryen_1 ?= { #Aerys II Targaryen crown inheritance
		if = {
			limit = {
				current_date >= 8262.1.1 #Aerys II ascends the throne and commissions the crown
				current_date < 8283.6.1 #Aerys is killed
			}
			create_artifact_asoiaf_aerys_II_crown_effect_historical = { OWNER = this }
			trigger_event = { id = asoiaf_equip_crown_events.8 days = 1 } #equip Aerys II's crown with delay because of overlapping effects
		}
	}
	character:Baratheon_2 ?= { #Robert I Baratheon; Aerys II crown inheritance
		if = {
			limit = {
				current_date = 8283.6.1 #Robert inherits the crown via taking the iron throne (gives it to Stannis the next day)
			}
			create_artifact_asoiaf_aerys_II_crown_effect_historical = { OWNER = this }
		}
	}
	character:Baratheon_3 ?= { #Stannis Baratheon; Aerys II crown inheritance
		if = {
			limit = {
				current_date >= 8283.6.2 #Stannis is given the crown and wears it later as king
			}
			create_artifact_asoiaf_aerys_II_crown_effect_historical = { OWNER = this }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				current_date >= 8299.1.4 #Stannis declares himself king
			}
			asoiaf_equip_aerys_II_crown_artefact_effect = yes #equip Aerys II's crown
		}
	}
	character:Baratheon_2 ?= { #Robert I Baratheon; Robert I crown inheritance
		if = {
			limit = {
				current_date >= 8284.6.1 #creation date for vanilla AGOT's Robert I crown, and also for AGOT+'s alternate version
				has_game_rule = asoiaf_new_dnas_stormlands_rule_on #replace with stormlands clothes rule once you've got actual outfits to trigger alongside it
			}
			create_artifact_asoiaf_robert_I_crown_effect = { OWNER = this }
			trigger_event = { id = asoiaf_setup_events.5 days = 1 } #destroy vanilla AGOT's Robert I crown with delay because of overlapping effects
			trigger_event = { id = asoiaf_setup_events.4 days = 1 } #equip Robert I's crown with delay because of overlapping effects
		}
	}
	character:Baratheon_5 ?= { #Joffrey I Baratheon; Robert I crown inheritance
		if = {
			limit = {
				current_date >= 8298.10.28 #Robert I dies and the crown passes to Joffrey
				has_game_rule = asoiaf_new_dnas_stormlands_rule_on #replace with stormlands clothes rule once you've got actual outfits to trigger alongside it
			}
			create_artifact_asoiaf_robert_I_crown_effect = { OWNER = this }
			trigger_event = { id = asoiaf_setup_events.5 days = 1 } #destroy vanilla AGOT's Robert I crown with delay because of overlapping effects
		}
	}
	character:Baratheon_7 ?= { #Tommen I Baratheon; Robert I crown inheritance
		if = {
			limit = {
				current_date >= 8300.1.1 #Joffrey I dies and the crown passes to Tommen
				has_game_rule = asoiaf_new_dnas_stormlands_rule_on #replace with stormlands clothes rule once you've got actual outfits to trigger alongside it
			}
			create_artifact_asoiaf_robert_I_crown_effect = { OWNER = this }

asoiaf_got_names_effect = {
	character:Greyjoy_13 ?= { #Yara Greyjoy (daughter of Balon)
		change_first_name = Yara
	}
	character:Arryn_8 ?= { #Robin Arryn (son of Jon)
		change_first_name = Robin
	}
}

asoiaf_alternative_ages_cleanup_effect = {
	#clear childhood education focus
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_focus = education_diplomacy
				has_focus = education_martial
				has_focus = education_stewardship
				has_focus = education_learning
				has_focus = education_intrigue
			}
		}
		set_focus = no
	}
	#assign sexuality if blank
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_sexuality = none
		}
		set_sexuality = heterosexual
	}
	#clear all childhood traits
	asoiaf_clear_childhood_traits_effect = yes
	# Hostage reaches adulthood
	if = {
		limit = { is_hostage = yes }
		save_scope_as = hostage
		warden ?= {
			set_variable = {
				name = hook_chance
				value = scope:hostage.bp2_hostage_loyalty_hook_chance_value
			}
			trigger_event = {
				id = bp2_hostage_system.0200
				days = 5
			}
		}
	}
	#replace uncrowned child modifier with regular version
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_inactive_trait = not_had_coronation
			has_character_modifier = uncoronated_child_modifier
		}
		remove_character_modifier = uncoronated_child_modifier
		add_character_modifier = uncoronated_modifier
	}
	#remove stray guardians
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_relation = {
				type = guardian
				count > 0
			}
		}
		random_relation = {
			type = guardian
			save_scope_as = educator
		}
		wrap_up_education_effect = yes
	}
	#victim transforms into opinion modifier
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_relation = { type = victim count >= 1 }
		}
		random_relation = { type = victim save_scope_as = victim }
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = no }
			set_variable = {
				name = had_childhood_victim_variable
				value = scope:victim
			}
		}
		add_opinion = {
			modifier = childhood_victim
			target = scope:victim
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_relation_potential_rival = scope:victim }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_relation_potential_rival = scope:victim
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_relation = { type = victim count >= 1 }
			}
			remove_relation_victim = scope:victim
		}
	}
	#bully transforms into opinion modifier
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_relation = { type = bully count >= 1 }
		}
		random_relation = { type = bully save_scope_as = bully }
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = no }
			set_variable = {
				name = had_childhood_bully_variable
				value = scope:bully
			}
		}
		add_opinion = {
			modifier = childhood_bully
			target = scope:bully
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_relation_potential_rival = scope:bully }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_relation_potential_rival = scope:bully
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_relation = { type = bully count >= 1 }
			}
			remove_relation_bully = scope:bully
		}
	}
	#crush transforms into opinion modifier
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				any_relation = { type = crush count >= 1 }
				exists = var:unrequited_crush
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = var:unrequited_crush
			}
			var:unrequited_crush = {
				save_scope_as = crushed_crush
			}
			scope:crushed_crush = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_ai = no
					}
					set_variable = {
						name = had_childhood_crush_variable
						value = root
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_relation = { type = crush count >= 1 }
			}
			random_relation = {
				type = crush
				save_scope_as = crush
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				set_variable = {
					name = had_childhood_crush_variable
					value = scope:crush
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = scope:crush
			}
			save_scope_as = root_crush
			scope:crush = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_relation_crush = root
					}
					add_character_flag = crush_over
					trigger_event = {
						id = childhood.0999
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = var:unrequited_crush
			}
			save_scope_as = root_crush
			scope:crushed_crush = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_relation_crush = root
					}
					add_character_flag = crush_over
					add_character_flag = unrequited_crush
					trigger_event = {
						id = childhood.0999
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				exists = scope:crush
			}
			add_opinion = {
				modifier = childhood_crush
				target = scope:crush
			}
		}
		every_relation = {
			type = crush
			reverse_add_opinion = {
				modifier = childhood_crush
				target = root
			}
			root = {
				remove_relation_crush = prev
			}
		}
	}
}

asoiaf_setup_health_fertility_effect = {
	every_living_character = {
		limit = {
			NOR = {
				is_human = no
				has_trait = infertile
				has_trait = physique_bad_3
				has_trait = infirm
				has_trait = incapable
				AND = {
					exists = character:asoiaf_Hammer_2 #Hugh/Kat's daughter
					this = character:asoiaf_Hammer_2
				}
				AND = {
					exists = character:Targaryen_128 #Shaera Targaryen (daughter of Aegon V)
					this = character:Targaryen_128
				}
				AND = {
					exists = character:Targaryen_1 #Aerys II Targaryen
					this = character:Targaryen_1
					current_date > 8277.1.1 #after Viserys is born limit the children
				}
				AND = {
					exists = character:Targaryen_2 #Rhaella Targaryen (daughter of Jaehaerys II)
					this = character:Targaryen_2
					current_date > 8277.1.1 #after Viserys is born limit the children
				}
				#AND = {
				#	exists = character:Targaryen_3 #Rhaegar Targaryen (son of Aerys II)
				#	this = character:Targaryen_3
				#	current_date > 8282.1.1 #after Aegon is born limit the children
				#}
				#AND = { #disabled since the Canon Children system terminates her pregnancies with Robert automatically now
				#	exists = character:Lannister_6 #Cersei Lannister (daughter of Tywin)
				#	this = character:Lannister_6
				#	current_date > 8284.1.1
				#}
				AND = {
					exists = character:Baratheon_2 #Robert I Baratheon
					this = character:Baratheon_2
					current_date > 8284.1.1
				}
				AND = {
					exists = character:Lannister_129 #Tytos Lannister (son of Gerold)
					this = character:Lannister_129
					exists = character:Lannister_4 #Tygett is born
				}
				AND = {
					exists = character:Hightower_9 #Alerie Hightower (daughter of Leyton)
					this = character:Hightower_9
					current_date > 8284.1.1 #once Margaery is born limit the children
				}
			}
		}
		add_character_modifier = {
			modifier = asoiaf_fertility_health_boost
			years = 10
		}
	}
}

asoiaf_setup_coa_fixes_effect = {
	trigger_event = { id = asoiaf_setup_events.2 days = 1 }
}

asoiaf_alternative_dayne_sigil_effect = {
	dynasty:dynn_Dayne ?= { set_coa = dynn_Dayne_alt }
}

asoiaf_alternative_arryn_sigil_effect = {
	dynasty:dynn_Arryn ?= { set_coa = dynn_Arryn_alt }
	house:house_ArrynGT ?= { set_coa = house_ArrynGT_alt }
}

	if = {
		limit = { has_game_rule = asoiaf_hbo_velaryons_rule_on }
		character:Rosby_13 ?= { #Make Tanda Rosby a Summer Islander of a different dynasty
			change_first_name = Chatana
			set_mother = character:asoiaf_Corlys_grandmother
			set_father = character:asoiaf_Corlys_grandfather
			set_house =  character:asoiaf_Corlys_grandfather.house
			set_culture = character:asoiaf_Corlys_grandfather.culture
			set_character_faith = character:asoiaf_Corlys_grandfather.faith
			copy_inheritable_appearance_from = character:asoiaf_Corlys_grandmother

		}
		character:Velaryon_31 ?= { copy_inheritable_appearance_from = character:Velaryon_asoiaf_31_HBO }
